    {
      "cell_type": "markdown",
      "source": [
        "# 앙상블 평가"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "Xd1_wlplLxQ-"
      }
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "\"\"\"\n",
        "[Cell 25 최종] 앙상블: BERT(klue/bert-base) + LSTM\n",
        "- Colab에서 그래프 바로 표시\n",
        "- 파일 저장은 선택사항\n",
        "\"\"\"\n",
        "\n",
        "import numpy as np\n",
        "import pandas as pd\n",
        "from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, classification_report, confusion_matrix\n",
        "from scipy.stats import spearmanr\n",
        "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n",
        "import seaborn as sns\n",
        "import gc\n",
        "\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"🎯 앙상블 예측 (BERT + LSTM)\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "\n",
        "# 1. 데이터 로드\n",
        "print(\"\\n📂 데이터 로드 중...\")\n",
        "\n",
        "bert_probs = np.load('data/finbert_test_predictions.npy')\n",
        "y_true = np.load('data/finbert_test_labels.npy')\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"  ✅ BERT 예측: {bert_probs.shape}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "import tensorflow as tf\n",
        "lstm_model = tf.keras.models.load_model('models/lstm_classifier.h5')\n",
        "data = np.load('data/lstm_dataset.npz')\n",
        "X_test = data['X_test']\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"  ✅ LSTM 데이터: {X_test.shape}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "lstm_probs = lstm_model.predict(X_test, verbose=0)\n",
        "print(f\"  ✅ LSTM 예측: {lstm_probs.shape}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 크기 맞추기\n",
        "min_len = min(len(bert_probs), len(lstm_probs))\n",
        "bert_probs = bert_probs[:min_len]\n",
        "lstm_probs = lstm_probs[:min_len]\n",
        "y_true = y_true[:min_len]\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"\\n✅ 데이터 정렬: {min_len:,} samples\")\n",
        "\n",
        "del lstm_model, data\n",
        "gc.collect()\n",
        "\n",
        "# 2. 앙상블 가중평균\n",
        "print(\"\\n⚙️  앙상블 가중치 설정...\")\n",
        "\n",
        "w_bert = 0.6\n",
        "w_lstm = 0.4\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"  BERT:  {w_bert}\")\n",
        "print(f\"  LSTM:  {w_lstm}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "ensemble_probs = w_bert * bert_probs + w_lstm * lstm_probs\n",
        "\n",
        "bert_preds = np.argmax(bert_probs, axis=1)\n",
        "lstm_preds = np.argmax(lstm_probs, axis=1)\n",
        "ensemble_preds = np.argmax(ensemble_probs, axis=1)\n",
        "\n",
        "# 3. 성능 비교\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"📊 성능 비교\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "\n",
        "acc_bert = accuracy_score(y_true, bert_preds)\n",
        "acc_lstm = accuracy_score(y_true, lstm_preds)\n",
        "acc_ensemble = accuracy_score(y_true, ensemble_preds)\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"\\nAccuracy:\")\n",
        "print(f\"  BERT (klue/bert-base): {acc_bert:.4f}\")\n",
        "print(f\"  LSTM:                  {acc_lstm:.4f}\")\n",
        "print(f\"  Ensemble:              {acc_ensemble:.4f}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "improvement = acc_ensemble - max(acc_bert, acc_lstm)\n",
        "print(f\"\\n  개선: {improvement:+.4f}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "if improvement > 0:\n",
        "    print(f\"  ✅ 앙상블이 개별 모델보다 우수합니다!\")\n",
        "elif improvement > -0.01:\n",
        "    print(f\"  ⚠️  앙상블과 개별 모델 성능이 비슷합니다\")\n",
        "else:\n",
        "    print(f\"  ❌ 앙상블이 개별 모델보다 낮습니다\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 4. 분류 리포트\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"📋 BERT 분류 리포트 (klue/bert-base)\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(classification_report(\n",
        "    y_true, bert_preds,\n",
        "    target_names=['하락(0)', '중립(1)', '상승(2)'],\n",
        "    digits=3\n",
        "))\n",
        "\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"📋 LSTM 분류 리포트\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(classification_report(\n",
        "    y_true, lstm_preds,\n",
        "    target_names=['하락(0)', '중립(1)', '상승(2)'],\n",
        "    digits=3\n",
        "))\n",
        "\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"📋 앙상블 분류 리포트 (BERT + LSTM)\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(classification_report(\n",
        "    y_true, ensemble_preds,\n",
        "    target_names=['하락(0)', '중립(1)', '상승(2)'],\n",
        "    digits=3\n",
        "))\n",
        "\n",
        "# 5. Confusion Matrix 비교 (바로 표시)\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"📊 Confusion Matrix 비교\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "\n",
        "fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 3, figsize=(18, 5))\n",
        "\n",
        "models_info = [\n",
        "    (bert_preds, 'BERT\\n(klue/bert-base)'),\n",
        "    (lstm_preds, 'LSTM'),\n",
        "    (ensemble_preds, 'Ensemble\\n(BERT + LSTM)')\n",
        "]\n",
        "\n",
        "for idx, (preds, title) in enumerate(models_info):\n",
        "    cm = confusion_matrix(y_true, preds)\n",
        "    sns.heatmap(\n",
        "        cm, annot=True, fmt='d', cmap='Blues',\n",
        "        xticklabels=['하락', '중립', '상승'],\n",
        "        yticklabels=['하락', '중립', '상승'],\n",
        "        ax=axes[idx],\n",
        "        cbar_kws={'label': 'Count'}\n",
        "    )\n",
        "    axes[idx].set_title(f'{title}\\nAcc: {accuracy_score(y_true, preds):.3f}',\n",
        "                       fontsize=14, fontweight='bold')\n",
        "    axes[idx].set_ylabel('True', fontsize=12)\n",
        "    axes[idx].set_xlabel('Predicted', fontsize=12)\n",
        "\n",
        "plt.tight_layout()\n",
        "plt.show()  # ✅ 바로 표시!\n",
        "\n",
        "# 6. Information Coefficient\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"📈 Information Coefficient (알파 지표)\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "\n",
        "y_numeric = y_true - 1\n",
        "\n",
        "bert_expected = bert_probs[:, 0] * -1 + bert_probs[:, 2] * 1\n",
        "lstm_expected = lstm_probs[:, 0] * -1 + lstm_probs[:, 2] * 1\n",
        "ensemble_expected = ensemble_probs[:, 0] * -1 + ensemble_probs[:, 2] * 1\n",
        "\n",
        "ic_bert, p_bert = spearmanr(y_numeric, bert_expected)\n",
        "ic_lstm, p_lstm = spearmanr(y_numeric, lstm_expected)\n",
        "ic_ensemble, p_ens = spearmanr(y_numeric, ensemble_expected)\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"\\n  BERT:     IC = {ic_bert:.4f} (p-value: {p_bert:.4f})\")\n",
        "print(f\"  LSTM:     IC = {ic_lstm:.4f} (p-value: {p_lstm:.4f})\")\n",
        "print(f\"  Ensemble: IC = {ic_ensemble:.4f} (p-value: {p_ens:.4f})\")\n",
        "\n",
        "print(\"\\n  💡 IC 해석:\")\n",
        "if abs(ic_ensemble) > 0.05 and p_ens < 0.05:\n",
        "    print(f\"     ✅ 강한 예측력! (IC > 0.05, p < 0.05)\")\n",
        "elif abs(ic_ensemble) > 0.03 and p_ens < 0.05:\n",
        "    print(f\"     ✅ 유의미한 예측력 (IC > 0.03, p < 0.05)\")\n",
        "elif abs(ic_ensemble) > 0.02:\n",
        "    print(f\"     ⚠️  약한 예측력 (IC > 0.02)\")\n",
        "else:\n",
        "    print(f\"     ❌ 예측력 없음 (IC ≈ 0)\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 7. IC 비교 시각화 (바로 표시)\n",
        "print(\"\\n📊 IC 비교 그래프...\")\n",
        "\n",
        "fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n",
        "\n",
        "models = ['BERT', 'LSTM', 'Ensemble']\n",
        "ics = [ic_bert, ic_lstm, ic_ensemble]\n",
        "colors = ['#3498db', '#e74c3c', '#2ecc71']\n",
        "\n",
        "bars = ax.bar(models, ics, color=colors, alpha=0.7, edgecolor='black', linewidth=1.5)\n",
        "\n",
        "# 값 표시\n",
        "for bar, ic in zip(bars, ics):\n",
        "    height = bar.get_height()\n",
        "    ax.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width()/2., height,\n",
        "            f'{ic:.4f}',\n",
        "            ha='center', va='bottom', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')\n",
        "\n",
        "ax.axhline(y=0, color='gray', linestyle='--', linewidth=1, alpha=0.5)\n",
        "ax.set_ylabel('Information Coefficient', fontsize=12)\n",
        "ax.set_title('Information Coefficient 비교\\n(높을수록 예측력 우수)',\n",
        "             fontsize=14, fontweight='bold')\n",
        "ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='y')\n",
        "\n",
        "plt.tight_layout()\n",
        "plt.show()  # ✅ 바로 표시!\n",
        "\n",
        "# 8. 앙상블 성공 케이스\n",
        "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 80)\n",
        "print(\"🔍 앙상블이 개별 모델보다 우수한 케이스\")\n",
        "print(\"=\" * 80)\n",
        "\n",
        "label_names = {0: '하락', 1: '중립', 2: '상승'}\n",
        "success_cases = []\n",
        "\n",
        "for i in range(len(y_true)):\n",
        "    if (ensemble_preds[i] == y_true[i] and\n",
        "        (bert_preds[i] != y_true[i] or lstm_preds[i] != y_true[i])):\n",
        "        success_cases.append(i)\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"\\n발견된 케이스: {len(success_cases):,}개\")\n",
        "print(f\"전체 대비: {len(success_cases)/len(y_true)*100:.1f}%\")\n",
        "\n",
        "if len(success_cases) > 0:\n",
        "    print(f\"\\n처음 3개 케이스:\")\n",
        "\n",
        "    for idx in success_cases[:3]:\n",
        "        print(f\"\\n📌 샘플 {idx+1}:\")\n",
        "        print(f\"  True:     {y_true[idx]} ({label_names[y_true[idx]]})\")\n",
        "        print(f\"  BERT:     {bert_preds[idx]} ({label_names[bert_preds[idx]]}) {'✅' if bert_preds[idx]==y_true[idx] else '❌'}\")\n",
        "        print(f\"  LSTM:     {lstm_preds[idx]} ({label_names[lstm_preds[idx]]}) {'✅' if lstm_preds[idx]==y_true[idx] else '❌'}\")\n",
        "        print(f\"  Ensemble: {ensemble_preds[idx]} ({label_names[ensemble_preds[idx]]}) ✅\")\n",
        "        print(f\"  확률:\")\n",
        "        print(f\"    BERT:     하락 {bert_probs[idx][0]:.2f} | 중립 {bert_probs[idx][1]:.2f} | 상승 {bert_probs[idx][2]:.2f}\")\n",
        "        print(f\"    LSTM:     하락 {lstm_probs[idx][0]:.2f} | 중립 {lstm_probs[idx][1]:.2f} | 상승 {lstm_probs[idx][2]:.2f}\")\n",
        "        print(f\"    Ensemble: 하락 {ensemble_probs[idx][0]:.2f} | 중립 {ensemble_probs[idx][1]:.2f} | 상승 {ensemble_probs[idx][2]:.2f}\")\n",
        "else:\n",
        "    print(\"\\n  → 앙상블의 추가 이득이 없습니다\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 9. 최종 요약 테이블\n",
